***gunnen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gunnen.html>gunnen</a> (9642)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gunnen.html>gunnen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*giunnan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gaunnaną</i>, a prefixed form of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*unnaną</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">gönnen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gunnen.html>gunnen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with indirect object</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to think someone deserves something, to witness or acknowledge someone's success or enjoyment without envy or grudge <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually referring to positive outcomes</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><b>2012</b>, Natasja Oosterloo, <i>Twitter <a href = vnd.unilang:jezelf.html>jezelf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:baan.html>baan</a></i>, page 37.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> gunfactor <a href = vnd.unilang:zorgt.html>zorgt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ervoor.html>ervoor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:positief.html>positief</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:denken.html>denken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daardoor.html>daardoor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gunnen.html>gunnen</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Likeability ensures that people think positively about you and because of that they <b>will be <a href = vnd.unilang:okay.html>okay</a> with</b> you <b>getting</b> something <b>nice</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gegund.html>gegund</a></b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You really <b>deserved</b> it!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gunt.html>gunt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:jou.html>jou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:functie.html>functie</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b>thinks</b> you <b>deserved</b> that position.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:misgunnen.html>misgunnen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with indirect object</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to award, to grant <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of <a href = vnd.unilang:orders.html>orders</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:tenders.html>tenders</a>, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><b>2005</b>, <i>Aanbestedingsreglement <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a> 2005: ARW 2005</i>, page 201.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> aanbesteder <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verplicht.html>verplicht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opdracht.html>opdracht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gunnen.html>gunnen</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The contracting party <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not required to <b>grant</b> the order.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bestuur.html>bestuur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:besprak.html>besprak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>wie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opdracht.html>opdracht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>zou</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gunnen.html>gunnen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The managing board <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> discussing to whom they would <b>award</b> the order.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with indirect object</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give, usually out of benevolence or <a href = vnd.unilang:grace.html>grace</a>; to grant
<ul><li><b>1741</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:johannes.html>Johannes</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muller.html>Muller</a>, <i>Absolutum decretum, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:volstrekt.html>Volstrekt</a> raadbesluyt <a href = vnd.unilang:gods.html>Gods</a></i>, page 17.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> groote <a href = vnd.unilang:koning.html>Koning</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gunde.html>gunde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a> genoodigde <a href = vnd.unilang:gasten.html>gasten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:genot.html>genot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> bruyloft; tendien eynde <a href = vnd.unilang:liet.html>liet</a> hy <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> noodigen.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The great King <b>granted</b> the pleasure of the wedding to all invited guests; to that end he let them be invited.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2011</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:stacy.html>Stacy</a> Schiff, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:cleopatra.html>Cleopatra</a></i>, Ambo (publ.).
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moederschap.html>moederschap</a> <a href = <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gunst.html>gunst</a> (2749)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gunst.html>gunst</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gonst.html>gonst</a></i>, prefixed from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ge-</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">onst</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">onste</i>, the latter from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">anst</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*unstiz</i>.
Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gunnen.html>gunnen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-st</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gunst.html>gunst</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gunsten.html>gunsten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gunst.html>gunstje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>favour</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gunst.html>gunst</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">formal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> somewhat dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">good grief</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">gosh</span></li></ol>

***gunsteling.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gunsteling.html>gunsteling</a> (60807)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gunst.html>gunst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">favour, benefit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ling</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gunsteling.html>gunsteling</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gunstelingen.html>gunstelingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gunsteling.html>gunstelingetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">beneficiary</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">someone who receives a favour or benefits</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***gup.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gup.html>gup</a> (105833)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gup.html>gup</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="common gender">c</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gup.html>guppen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:guppy.html>guppy</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">gupje</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:guppie.html>guppie</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γυμνασία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gumnasía</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">athletic training, exercise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γυμνός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gumnós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">naked</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, because Greek athletes <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> training naked.

***gyro.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gyro.html>gyro</a> (82971)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally a shortening of gyroscope.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gyro.html>gyro</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gyros</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A gyroscope</li>
<li>A gyrocompass</li>
<li>An autogyro</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Greek language">Greek</a></span> <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">γύρος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gýros</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; from the turning of the meat on a spit. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">gyre</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gyrus.html>gyrus</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gyro.html>gyro</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gyros</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A style of Greek sandwich commonly filled with grilled meat, tomato, onions, and tzatziki sauce.
<dl><dd><i>I'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> have a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gyro.html>gyro</a></b>, please.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The correct pronunciation of this word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> disputed. The pronunciation <span class="IPA">/ˈdʒaɪɹoʊ/</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often proscribed. All of the listed pronunciations may be found in use. (The modern Greek pronunciation <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <span class="IPA">/ˈʝiɾos/</span>.):
</p>
<ul><li><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r50165410"/></li></ul>
</body>

***gyrus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gyrus.html>gyrus</a> (82969)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gȳrus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">circle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γῦρος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gûros</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gyro.html>gyro</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">gyre</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gyrus.html>gyrus</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gyri</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gyruses</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A ridge or fold on the cerebral cortex.</li></ol>
</body>

***haag.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:haag.html>haag</a> (49404)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hāge</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">haghe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hago</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*hagō</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hagô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hedge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kaghon</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>haw</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haag.html>haag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hagen.html>hagen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haag.html>haagje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A hedge, thicket of <a href = vnd.unilang:woody.html>woody</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bushes.html>bushes</a> planted in a row</li>
<li>A lane, (often double) row of lined-up persons or <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a>, as for a formal guard of honor inspection</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Undergrowth, a dense low forest</li></ol>

***haai.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:haai.html>haai</a> (4943)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">haeye</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">há-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shark</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with the /j/ appearing influenced by the declined forms /hajə(n)/. Probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hanh-u-</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">haj</i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:hai.html>Hai</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haai.html>haai</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haaien.html>haaien</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haai.html>haaitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Caribbean_reef_shark.jpg/250px-Caribbean_reef_shark.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="156" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Caribbean_reef_shark.jpg/375px-Caribbean_reef_shark.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Caribbean_reef_shark.jpg/500px-Caribbean_reef_shark.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1968" data-file-height="1228" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><i>Caribische rifhaai</i><br />Caribbean Reef Shark</div></div></div>
<ol><li>shark, fish of the superorder Selachimorpha (sometimes also including certain extinct shark-like members of the Elasmobranchii outside this superorder)</li>
<li>greedy person</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:vissen.html>vissen</a>)</span> kraakbenige <a href = vnd.unilang:roofvis.html>roofvis</a> <sup id="cite_ref-qhaai1_2-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-qhaai1-2"> | 2 | </a></sup></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:haak.html>haak</a> (3975)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hāke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hako</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hakô</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haak.html>haak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haken.html>haken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haakje.html>haakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>hook</li>
<li>bracket (for enclosing text or mathematical symbols)</li></ol>

***haan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:haan.html>haan</a> (8859)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hane</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hano</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hanô</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kan-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hahn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">hane</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haan.html>haan</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hanen.html>hanen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haantje.html>haantje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A cock, a <a href = vnd.unilang:rooster.html>rooster</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">male chicken</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li>The male of various other species of gallinaceous <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a>.</li>
<li>The lock or hammer of an older type of firearm.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:haan.html>haan</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:vogels.html>vogels</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:mannelijk.html>mannelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> hoenderachtige <a href = vnd.unilang:vogels.html>vogels</a>

***haar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> (56)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">haer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:hiro.html>hiro</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hezōi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">personal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Third-person singular, feminine object pronoun: her
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeg.html>zeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></b> (1), <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunt.html>kunt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></b> (2) <a href = vnd.unilang:beter.html>beter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> mailtje <a href = vnd.unilang:sturen.html>sturen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I’<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> mention it to <b>her</b>, but you’d better send <b>her</b> a mail as well.</span></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>(1) accusative personal pronoun, (2) dative personal pronoun</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heur.html>heur</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">archaic or dialectal variant</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3_2">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">haer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:hiro.html>hiro</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hezǫ̂</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner_3">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></strong> (<i>dependent possessive, independent possive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hare.html>hare</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Third-person plural possessive adjective: their</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>Haar</a></i> (“their”) <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the normal Middle Dutch form for all genders in the plural. In modern Dutch, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></i> successively replaced <i><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></i> in this function. Some writers of the 19th and early 20th century made a learned distinction, using <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></i> as the masculine and neuter plural, but <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></i> for the feminine in both singular and plural: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:mannen.html>mannen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hunne.html>hunne</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouwen.html>vrouwen</a></i> (“men and their wives”) versus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vrouwen.html>vrouwen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hare.html>hare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mannen.html>mannen</a></i> (“women and their husbands”).</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">their</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4_2">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hâer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hār</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hērą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> or <abbr title="common gender">c</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haren.html>haren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haartje.html>haartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">hair</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">collection of hairs</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">hair</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">mammalian keratin filament</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The noun <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> traditionally neuter in all senses. As a countable noun, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now sometimes of common gender.</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Persoonlijk_voornaamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:persoonlijk.html>Persoonlijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voornaamwoord.html>voornaamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></b>
</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haarspeld.html>haarspeld</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bocht.html>bocht</a></i>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hairpin turn</i>; in the oldest use referring to a turn by an aeroplane.

***haas.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:haas.html>haas</a> (14138)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hāse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*haso</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hasô</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haas.html>haas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hazen.html>hazen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haasje.html>haasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:hare.html>hare</a>, lagomorph of the genus <i>Lepus</i></li>
<li>meat of the <a href = vnd.unilang:hare.html>hare</a>, fillet</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rabbit, pacesetter <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">runner in a distance race who <a href = vnd.unilang:sets.html>sets</a> the pace</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">haessen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hāsenewa</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hāhsenewa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hanhsenwō</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hanhasenwō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> tendon, Achilles tendon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hanhaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*senwō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sinew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hataz</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:haat.html>haat</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hass</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hate</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a></i>.

***haben.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:haben.html>haben</a> (105797)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:haben.html>haben</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">habēn</i> (Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">hebbian</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hafa</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">hava</i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href = vnd.unilang:ha.html>ha</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">habba</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌷𐌰𐌱𐌰𐌽</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">haban</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">habban</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*habbjan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*habjaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*keh₂p-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grasp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">have</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">have</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:haben.html>haben</a></strong> (<i>irregular</i>, <i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de">hat</b>, <i>past tense</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de">hatte</b>, <i>past participle</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de">gehabt</b>, <i>past subjunctive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de">hätte</b>, <i>auxiliary</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:haben.html>haben</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with a past participle</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have (<span class="use-with-mention">forms the <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> and past <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> tense</span>)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have; to own <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to possess, have ownership of; to possess a certain characteristic</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have; to hold <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to contain within itself/oneself</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Glaub und <b>hab</b> keine <a href = vnd.unilang:angst.html>Angst</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Believe and don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> be afraid <i>or</i> Believe and <b>have</b> no fear.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have, get <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to obtain, acquire</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to receive</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to be scheduled to attend</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to be afflicted with, suffer from</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of units of measure</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to contain, be composed of, equal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Ein <a href = vnd.unilang:meter.html>Meter</a> <b>hat</b> 100 Zentimeter.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">There are 100 centimetres in one metre.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">One metre <b><a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a></b> 100 centimetres.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i>es</i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> there be, there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, there are
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Es <b>hat</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zwei.html>zwei</a> Bücher.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">There are two books.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make a fuss
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><b>Hab</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dich.html>dich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nicht.html>nicht</a> so!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> make such a fuss!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">es</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">mit</i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be occupied with, to like
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Ich <b>hab'</b>s nich so mit Hunden.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm not a great fan of dogs.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">I don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>have</b> it that much with dogs.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***hacienda.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hacienda.html>hacienda</a> (31194)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:hacienda.html>hacienda</a></i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">faena</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fazenda</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hacienda.html>hacienda</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">haciendas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A large homestead in a <a href = vnd.unilang:ranch.html>ranch</a> or estate usually in <a href = vnd.unilang:places.html>places</a> where Colonial Spanish culture <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> architectural influence.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1907</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harold_Edward_Bindloss" class="extiw" title="w:Harold Edward Bindloss">Harold Bindloss</a>,  chapter 14, in  <cite>The Dust of Conflict</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL4429277W">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The hot day <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>, and the light failing rapidly, when Appleby, who <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> just finished comida, <a href = vnd.unilang:sat.html>sat</a> by a window of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hacienda.html>hacienda</a></b> San Cristoval with an English newspaper upon his knee.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***hag.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hag.html>hag</a> (69735)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">hagge</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">hegge</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:demon.html>demon</a>, old woman</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, shortening of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hægtesse</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hægtes</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">harpy, witch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hagatusjō</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian language">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">Häkse</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">witch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heks.html>heks</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hexe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">witch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), compounds of (1) <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hagaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">able, skilled</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hagr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">handy, skillful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">behac</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pleasurable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱak-</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">शक्नोति</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">śaknóti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">he can</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>),<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> and (2) <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tusjǭ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">witch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare dialectal Norwegian <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">tysja</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fairy, she-elf</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hag.html>hag</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hags</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A witch, sorceress, or enchantress; a wizard.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1565</b>,  Arthur Golding (tr.),  <cite>The Fyrst Fower Bookes of P. Ouidius Nasos worke intitled Metamorphosis</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://gateway.proquest.com/openurl?ctx_ver=Z39.88-2003amp;res_id=xri:eeboamp;rft_id=xri:eebo:image:10762:44">[1]</a></sup>, London |  William Seres, The Fovrthe Booke:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">And that olde <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hag.html>hag</a></b> that with a staffe his staggering lymbes dooth stay</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1851</b> November 14,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Herman_Melville" class="extiw" title="w:Herman Melville">Herman Melville</a>,  chapter 3, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moby-Dick" class="extiw" title="w:Moby-Dick">Moby-Dick; or, The Whale</a></cite>, 1st American edition, New York, N.Y. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harper_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:Harper (publisher)">Harper amp; Brothers</a>; London: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Richard_Bentley_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:Richard Bentley (publisher)">Richard Bentley</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/57395299">57395299</a></small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Such unaccountable masses of shades and <a href = vnd.unilang:shadows.html>shadows</a>, that at first you almost thought some ambitious young artist, in the time of the New England <b>hags</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> endeavored to delineate <a href = vnd.unilang:chaos.html>chaos</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bewitched.html>bewitched</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An ugly old woman.</li>
<li>A fury; a she-monster.
<ul><li><b>1646</b>, Richard Crashaw, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:steps.html>Steps</a> to the Temple</i>, “Sospetto D' Herode”, stanza 37:
<dl><dd>Fourth of the cursed knot of <b>hags</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> she / Or rather all the other three in one; / Hell's shop of slaughter she does oversee, / And still assist the execution</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A hagfish; one of various eel-like fish of the family Myxinidae, allied to the lamprey, with a suctorial mouth, labial appendages, and a single pair of gill openings.</li>
<li>A hagdon or shearwater; one of various sea <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a> of the genus <i>Puffinus</i>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An appearance of light and fire on a horse's <a href = vnd.unilang:manen.html>mane</a> or a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>'s hair.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1656</b>,  Thomas White,  <cite>Peripateticall Institutions</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://gateway.proquest.com/openurl?ctx_ver=Z39.88-2003amp;res_id=xri:eeboamp;rft_id=xri:eebo:image:115975:87">[2]</a></sup>, page 149:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><i>Flamma lambentes</i> (or those <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> call <i><b>Haggs</b></i>) are made of Sweat or some other Vapour issuing out of the Head; a not-unusuall sight amongst us when <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> ride by night in the Summer time: They are extinguisht, like flames, by shaking the Horse <a href = vnd.unilang:mains.html>Mains</a></span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>The fruit of the hagberry, <i>Prunus padus</i>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sleep paralysis</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">witch or sorceress</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> See Thesaurus:magician</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">ugly old woman</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> See Thesaurus:ugly woman</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">eel-like marine fish</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">borer</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">hagfish</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">sleepmarken</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">slime eel</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">sucker</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">myxinid</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">sea bird</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">hagdon</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">haglet</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">shearwater</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">fruit of the hagberry</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">bird cherry</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">hackberry</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a href = vnd.unilang:hag.html>hag</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hǫgg</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cut, gap, breach</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, derivative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hǫggva</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hack, hew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hew</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hag.html>hag</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hags</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A small wood, or part of a wood or copse, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> marked off or enclosed for felling, or which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> felled.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1845</b>,  Edward Fairfax (tr.),  <cite>Godfrey of Bulloigne; or, The Recovery of Jerusalem: Done into English Heroical Verse</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.worldcat.org/title/godfrey-of-bulloigne-or-the-recovery-of-jerusalem-done-into-english-heroical-verse/oclc/37660028">[3]</a></sup>, page 168:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">This <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a>, he <a href = vnd.unilang:led.html>led</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> hoults and <b>hags</b>; / Through thorns and <a href = vnd.unilang:bushes.html>bushes</a> scant my <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a> I <a href = vnd.unilang:drew.html>drew</a></span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A quagmire; mossy ground where peat or turf <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> cut.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1662</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> William Dugdale,  <cite>The History of Imbanking and Drayning of Divers Fenns and Marshes</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://quod.lib.umich.edu/e/eebo/A36795.0001.001">[4]</a></sup>, page 292:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">And they likewise ordained <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> that all the warp should be thrown into the Common wayes, to fill up <b>haggs</b> and lakes, where need <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>, upon a great penalty, where it should ly <a href = vnd.unilang:neer.html>neer</a> the Common <a href = vnd.unilang:rode.html>rode</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:hag.html>hag</a>(g)ōnan</i> (compare obsolete <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hagen.html>hagen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to torment, agonize</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">haga</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to tire, weaken</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hag.html>hag</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">hags</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hagging</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hagged</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To harass; to weary with vexation.

***hagelslag.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hagelslag.html>hagelslag</a> (51759)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hagelslach</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">severe hailstorm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hagel.html>hagel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hail</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slag.html>slag</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">blow, hit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. As a term for a type of sweet, it originally referred to elongated white aniseed <a href = vnd.unilang:sprinkles.html>sprinkles</a> as they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> thought to resemble falling hail; this sense <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> subsequently widened as other varieties entered the market.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hagelslag.html>hagelslag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>hundreds and thousands, <a href = vnd.unilang:sprinkles.html>sprinkles</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">elongated and often made of chocolate</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; jimmies <span class="defdate">[from early 20th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hagel.html>hagel</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hagelkorrel.html>hagelkorrel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>hailstorm, particularly a severe one</li></ol>
