***haggard.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:haggard.html>haggard</a> (35099)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:haggard.html>haggard</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">faulcon</i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">hagard</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wild falcon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> ( gt; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">hagard</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dazed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:hag.html>hag</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">coppice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> ( gt; archaic <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:hag.html>Hag</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hedge, grove</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>). Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*hagia</i> ( gt; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">haie</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hedge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>)<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:haggard.html>haggard</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:haggard.html>haggard</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:haggard.html>haggard</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:looking.html>Looking</a> exhausted, worried, or poor in condition
<ul><li><b>1685</b>, John Dryden, <i>The Despairing Lover</i>
<dl><dd>Staring his <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a>, and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:haggard.html>haggard</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> his look.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1851</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nathaniel_Hawthorne" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Nathaniel Hawthorne">Nathaniel Hawthorne</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_House_of_the_Seven_Gables" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The House of the Seven Gables">The House of the Seven <a href = vnd.unilang:gables.html>Gables</a></a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Then there <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a pale, care-wrinkled woman, not old, but <b><a href = vnd.unilang:haggard.html>haggard</a></b>, and already with streaks of gray among her hair, like silver ribbons; one of those women, naturally delicate, whom you at once recognize as worn to death by a brute—probably, a drunken brute—of a husband, and at least nine children.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1986</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_le_Carr%C3%A9" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John le Carré">John le Carré</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Perfect_Spy" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:A Perfect Spy">A <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>Perfect</a> Spy</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">By the end of two weeks there isn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> a county in England where he hasn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> pledged his holiness six different ways — which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not to deny that intermittently he <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> visions of himself as a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:haggard.html>haggard</a></b> apostle of the life renounced, converting beautiful women and millionaires to Christian poverty.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>Pale and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:haggard.html>haggard</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:faces.html>faces</a>.</i></dd>
<dd><i>A gradual descent into a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:haggard.html>haggard</a></b> and feeble state.</i></dd>
<dd><i>The years of hardship made her look somewhat <b><a href = vnd.unilang:haggard.html>haggard</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>Wild or untamed
<dl><dd><i>a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:haggard.html>haggard</a></b> or refractory hawk</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:haggard.html>haggard</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">haggards</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">falconry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A hunting bird captured as an <a href = vnd.unilang:adult.html>adult</a>.
<ul><li><b>1599</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>}, <i><a href="https://<a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a>.wikipedia.org/wiki/Much_Ado_About_Nothing" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Much Ado About Nothing">Much Ado About Nothing</a></i>, <a href="https://<a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a>.wikisource.org/wiki/Much_Ado_About_Nothing_(Shakespeare)" class="extiw" title="s:Much Ado About Nothing (Shakespeare)">Act 3 Scene 1</a>
<dl><dd>No, truly, Ursula, she is too disdainful;</dd>
<dd>I know her spirits are as coy and wild</dd>
<dd>As <b>haggards</b> of the rock.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">falconry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A young or untrained hawk or falcon.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A fierce, intractable creature.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1590–1592</b>,  <a href="https://<a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a>.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://<a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a>.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Taming_of_the_Shrew" class="extiw" title="w:The Taming of the Shrew">The Taming of the Shrew</a>”, in  <cite>Mr. William Shakespeares Comedies, Histories, amp; Tragedies: Published According to the True Originall Copies</cite> (<a href="https://<a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a>.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://<a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a>.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://<a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a>.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://<a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a>.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a <a href = vnd.unilang:rel.html>rel</a>="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act IV, scene ii]:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a>="<a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a>">I have loved this proud disdainful <b>haggard</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A hag.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can we find and add a quotation of Garth to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://<a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a>.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a>">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a>="non">heygarðr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hay-yard</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a>="<a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a>">haggard</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a>="<a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a>">haggards</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialect<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://<a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a>.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isle_of_Man" class="extiw" title="w:Isle of <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a>">Isle of Man</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://<a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a>.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ireland" class="extiw" title="w:Ireland">Ireland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://<a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a>.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A stackyard, an enclosure on a farm for stacking grain, hay, etc.

***hail.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> hail (6468)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p>[A] <b>hail</b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:aanroep.html>aanroep</a></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:roep.html>roep</a></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord_2"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p>[B] <b>hail</b>
